  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_8130f262-300c-407f-89e6-7cdd5f9b6697'
      });

      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer7440154849958018091">Kyon Ensin finally has what he’s always wanted: possession of Kricket Hollowell, the priestess who foresees the future. Together, their combined power will be unrivaled. Kricket, however, doesn’t crave the crown of Ethar—she has an unbreakable desire to live life on her own terms, a life that she desperately wants to share with her love, Trey Allairis.<br/><br/>As conspiracies rage </span>
  <span id="freeText7440154849958018091" style="display:none">Kyon Ensin finally has what he’s always wanted: possession of Kricket Hollowell, the priestess who foresees the future. Together, their combined power will be unrivaled. Kricket, however, doesn’t crave the crown of Ethar—she has an unbreakable desire to live life on her own terms, a life that she desperately wants to share with her love, Trey Allairis.<br /><br />As conspiracies rage in the war for Ethar, Kricket’s so-called allies want to use her as a spy. Even those held closest cannot be trusted—including Astrid, her sister, and Giffen, a member of a mysterious order with a hidden agenda. But Kricket’s resolve will not allow her to be used as anyone’s pawn, even as the Brotherhood sharpens its plans to cut out her heart.<br /><br />As the destiny prophesied by her mother approaches, Kricket will backtrack through her fiery future to reshape it. For she knows one thing above all else: the only person she can truly count on is herself.</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=2015-reads">2015-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=abusive-boyfriends">abusive-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=serve-me-up-insta-love">serve-me-up-insta-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1402337661" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11871936727150391399">Warning: spoilers. <br/><br/>Absolutely no stars. <br/><br/>I know a lot of people might be confused why I decided to continue this series despite disliking each book along the way. I get that it might seem pointless to subject myself to mediocrity purposefully. But I'll be honest, a small part of myself enjoyed the terribleness in a sense of morbid fascination. <br/><br/>Without a doubt, Darken the Stars is the worst of the three and actually angered me. While books one and two can be swept under the rug as simple wish fulf</span>
  <span id="freeText11871936727150391399" style="display:none">Warning: spoilers. <br /><br />Absolutely no stars. <br /><br />I know a lot of people might be confused why I decided to continue this series despite disliking each book along the way. I get that it might seem pointless to subject myself to mediocrity purposefully. But I'll be honest, a small part of myself enjoyed the terribleness in a sense of morbid fascination. <br /><br />Without a doubt, Darken the Stars is the worst of the three and actually angered me. While books one and two can be swept under the rug as simple wish fulfillment gone terribly wrong, this one is a flaming pile of dog shit. <br /><br />I didn't really have any intention of reviewing Darken the Stars, but after browsing other reviews, I feel morally obligated to say what no one is talking about. Kricket falls in love with the primary antagonist of the series -- the guy, who at one point, tries to choke her under water into submission. I'm not talking about a poorly written Stockholm syndrome. This is a legitimate romance that the author attempts to sell the reading on and it's so horribly offensive. <br /><br />The entire novel is based around Kricket finally being in the palm of Kyon's hands, right where he wants her. She's trapped on his beach and makes several attempts at escape with no success. Each time she does try to fight Kyon, he hurts her in some way. He also chooses what she wears and makes it clear that her opinions and wants mean nothing. Basically, he's disgusting and the farthest thing from romantic. <br /><br />However, somewhere along the lines, Kricket starts to fall for Kyon by way of a forced alliance (of course) and "changes" him. This is so very problematic. First, it completely glosses over the severity of domestic abuse. Second, you can't FIX people, certainly not abusers, with love. Out of the blue Kyon starts showing affection and a little more respect for Kricket. Then we find out that her mother entrusted Kyon to look after Kricket, which is supposed to explain why he sought after her so hard in the first two books. Kricket accepts this and starts to rationalize some of his abusive tendencies and dismiss the others. There's even a point in the book where she refers to him as "my psychopath." Also, there's a lot of sex between them, where Kyon insists on getting Kricket to confess her love as he pounds into her. &gt;insert vomiting&lt;<br /><br />What's worst is how so many reviewers are so pro Kyon as a love interest and it's got me going HUH? I'm not the kind of person that is usually bothered by how others react to books, but in cases like this, it really disturbs me to see it. And I think it's entirely irresponsible for an author to portray an abusive relationship as romantic. It's sick. <br /><br />Side note: this entire series revolves around the mental, emotional, and physical abuse of one female character by way of the people who supposedly love her. Who the hell thought this was a good idea? <br /><br />Anyway, this is a case where my curiosity really did me no good. But I just had to know how it ended and the fact that it was free on Kindle Unlimited didn't help. Next time I'll try to remember that just because I CAN, doesn't mean I SHOULD. I definitely don't recommend this, not even for the lols. Stay far away. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11871936727150391399" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1349248437" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1349248437" />
    <a title="Tara" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10575548-tara"><img alt="Tara" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1448732990p2/10575548.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1349248437?book_show_action=true">Jul 29, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tara" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tara" href="/user/show/10575548-tara">Tara</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10575548-tara?shelf=strong-alpha-male">strong-alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10575548-tara?shelf=heart-wrenching-soul-crushing">heart-wrenching-soul-crushing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10575548-tara?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10575548-tara?shelf=love-triangle">love-triangle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10575548-tara?shelf=strong-female">strong-female</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10575548-tara?shelf=enemies-to-lovers">enemies-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10575548-tara?shelf=forbidden-romance">forbidden-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1349248437" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15100267718752333069">I’m actually really heartbroken over writing this review. I keep wavering back and forth between wanting to give it one star and wanting to give it five. Between anger and despair. Between hate and heartbreaking love. Why have you done this to me, Amy?! Why?<br/><br/>I was so invested, so in love, so ready to hand Amy Bartol my heart encased in glass like a trophy, hers to hold forever, because she had rightfully earned it. And then with one book in this series, really even with the final 35% of the book,</span>
  <span id="freeText15100267718752333069" style="display:none">I’m actually really heartbroken over writing this review. I keep wavering back and forth between wanting to give it one star and wanting to give it five. Between anger and despair. Between hate and heartbreaking love. Why have you done this to me, Amy?! Why?<br /><br />I was so invested, so in love, so ready to hand Amy Bartol my heart encased in glass like a trophy, hers to hold forever, because she had rightfully earned it. And then with one book in this series, really even with the final 35% of the book, she completely shattered that heart. I feel betrayed. <br /><br />I’m so conflicted. On one hand, I kind of understand the ending. It makes sense in a way because of Kricket’s character. And on the other hand, she deserved so much better! I feel so let down. So much of the series set me up to fall in love with certain characters and hate others, only to have that used against me as a weapon. I feel battered and bruised and slightly broken.<br /><br />I have to say, this is the first time I ever want to give a conditional rating on a book. If this is the final book, I’m so angry that I’m inclined to give it one star. If there will be another, I have enough hope to give it a five simply for the emotions it evoked and the unique and innovative storyline. I’m conservatively giving it three. It’s right in the middle and only fair.<br /><br />There’s no denying that Amy’s imagination and storytelling ability is impeccable. I mean really, truly flawless. I was on the edge of my seat through most of this series and so in awe. She wields words like a weapon and unfortunately, they damn near killed me with this one.<br /><br />I really sincerely hope that there is another book. I feel like there are so many loose ends, so many unanswered questions, so much left that needs to happen. I don’t feel any sort of closure at all, in any sense of the word. I so wanted this to be more than it was. How can this be so epically beautiful and tragic and disappointing at the same time? <i>Please, Amy!</i> This is me on my knees. I’m actually sitting on my knees as I type this. <i>Please</i> write another book! Please give this strong, courageous, beautiful character an ending the likes of which she deserves. My God, she’s earned it! Amy Bartol didn't just darken the stars, she darkened my fucking heart!<br /><br />I received this book from the publisher via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review.<br /><br /><b>Edited to add:</b> I have to downgrade my review from 3 stars to 2 stars. It's been more than a month and I'm still angry over this book. I feel completely cheated. The first two books ended up on my "All Time Favorites" shelf and this book completely destroyed the series. I don't remember ever feeling so let down. I may revisit this review for a third time if the author ever publishes another book in the series but if this is truly the end, I could not be more disappointed.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15100267718752333069" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1270198906" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1270198906" />
    <a title="Angela" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30035966-angela"><img alt="Angela" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1523817330p2/30035966.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1270198906?book_show_action=true">May 02, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela" href="/user/show/30035966-angela">Angela</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30035966-angela?shelf=floating-or-falling">floating-or-falling</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30035966-angela?shelf=badass-females">badass-females</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30035966-angela?shelf=5-star-favorites">5-star-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1270198906" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8243886000508444668"><b>
  <i>"Deep down, however, I fear that I've come to love a lie." </i>
  <i>  </i>
</b><br/>Thanks Amy, for confusing the crap out of me... my heart doesn't know what direction it wants to go in. This book messed with my head for multiple different reasons.<br/><br/>When I finished<i> <a href='http://southernbredsouthernread.blogspot.com/2015/04/sea-of-stars-by-amy-bartol_3.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sea of Stars</a></i> I was 100% team Trey. Now that I have finished <i>Darken the Stars </i>I'm so torn between Trey and Kyon... Actually I might not be?!? Ugh I truly don't know where to start! Trey, Kyon, Kricket... I'm a glass case of emotions! Much like I did wi</span>
  <span id="freeText8243886000508444668" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>"Deep down, however, I fear that I've come to love a lie." </i>
  <i>  </i>
</b><br>Thanks Amy, for confusing the crap out of me... my heart doesn't know what direction it wants to go in. This book messed with my head for multiple different reasons.<br><br>When I finished<i> <a href="http://southernbredsouthernread.blogspot.com/2015/04/sea-of-stars-by-amy-bartol_3.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Sea of Stars</a></i> I was 100% team Trey. Now that I have finished <i>Darken the Stars </i>I'm so torn between Trey and Kyon... Actually I might not be?!? Ugh I truly don't know where to start! Trey, Kyon, Kricket... I'm a glass case of emotions! Much like I did with my <a href="http://southernbredsouthernread.blogspot.com/2015/09/queen-of-shadows-by-sarah-j-maas.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <i>Queen of Shadows</i>
</a> review I'm going to do a lot more talking about characters than I am about plot.<br><br>I'm not going to lie to you or beat around the bush with this.... We get a lot less Trey in this book than I was ever expecting... and at first this had me super peeved. I was mad that all our free time wasn't again filled with stolen moments and forbidden romance. Needless to say I was a little bit huffy the first few chapters in. That was until it dawned on me that if Amy gave me all the things I "wanted" then it was would be book two repeated and that what I really wanted was something different and new for this series. I got it too.<br><br>Trey was just Trey in this book. As much as I still wanted more of him I was again still thankful for what we got instead. He's still seems just as sexy and strong as ever... but he is still the same Trey. The man that thinks he has to stand in front of Kricket instead of besides her as equals. <i>Darken the Stars </i>is more about Kyon and Kricket's story. Yes, you heard right; <b>WE GET A LOT OF KYON!!! Never thought I'd be excited to say that.</b> I'll get to that in a minute though... Kricket is still the whip smart fire cracker that we got in the first two books, but in this one shes a little more vulnerable and dare I say more like-able. Don't get me wrong, I liked her in the previous books, but I liked getting so see the raw more emotional side of her. We get to see more into her thought process and how seeing into the future really effects her. I like her wits over fist persona and her strong will to fight for what she wants. Not what the world needs but for what she needs. Some might think that comment sounds rather selfish for a leading lady, but in my eyes it's refreshing. Then there's Kyon. Everyone from here to Mars knows I love the villains. I always swoon over the bad boy... and what's better than your average bad boy? The bad boy who knows he's bad and doesn't care to be anything else! He owns it. Kyon has the same thing going for him that Warner from <a href="http://southernbredsouthernread.blogspot.com/2015/02/revisit-book-shatter-me-by-tahereh-mafi.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">The Shatter Me Trilogy</a> has. At first ya boy is beyond creepy and clingy and you're biggest worry is when and where he is going to make a skin suit out of Kricket. As time goes on though you start to see why he is the way he is. That he might be the "villain" but that he gives something to Kricket that no one else has. I also want to mention how I loved how he wants to teach Kricket things. He want to confide in her, and also sees her as an equal. He was the biggest surprise in this book for me. He becomes charming, jokey, romantic, fierce, he's always man-handling someone, he doesn't wear a shirt often.... <b>and holy hot half-breed I just want to lick his face... and that seafood dinner scene</b>... Whoosh, sorry. Excuse me. Got caught I up in the moment.<br><br><i>"Courage is a value that you hold dear. You live for <br>danger... I can't avoid danger. There's a difference... No. You slap <br>danger in the face and wait for it to react." </i><br><br><i>Darken the Stars </i>plot does take a slower pace than the two previous. The first two are all about action packed Wtf moments and chase scenes while this one is more about answering the unanswered questions we had from the others. It's about giving us more of a world history and character development. Also I don't know if I'm the only one whose going to think this, but whatever, I think the plot for<i> DTS </i>is a lot darker as well which I found to be a plus... I don't even want to get into how my number one biggest fears is present in this book. When that bomb gets dropped I almost threw up from being terrified. I'm not even going to mention what it is because I do feel like it's a little bit of a spoiler, but if you know me at all, then you'll already know what it is... because again <b>it's number one on my list of biggest fears. Just shuttering thinking about it again.<i> </i></b><i>DTS</i> is more a book that is set into place to set things up for the further installments in the series. The pace really doesn't pick up till closer to the end and takes several turns that I didn't except... And that ending! I just have no idea where this book is headed, what will come in the future, and this has me both stressed and very excited.<br><br><div>
  <br>
  <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-DIVWI3TDrsY/VfBramnuqsI/AAAAAAAACRQ/0zzSo658Ix0/s1600/stressed.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441819756ra/16156095.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</div><br><br><b>Sigh. There's going to be no other way for me to get over this book hangover that <i>Darken the Stars</i> has given me than watch really low rated movies on Netflix and binge on Ben and Jerry's. Goodbye cruel world.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="8243886000508444668" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1349591001" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8823710736700004173"><i> I received this ARC from 47North Amazon Publishing Via NG in return for an honest review.</i><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Deep down, however, I fear that I’ve come to love a lie.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>Bruised…battered….gutted…in shock. Those are my feelings right now!</b><br/><br/>Amy Bartol I’m breaking up with you<br/><br/>You led me astray.<br/><br/>You gave me mixed signals.<br/><br/>I trusted you!<br/><br/>I trusted you with my heart and you smashed it with your words. <br/><br/>How could you?<br/><br/>If we were married, I’d want a divorce.<br/><br/>How could you take away the boys? How could you take Jax, Trey and Wayr</span>
  <span id="freeText8823710736700004173" style="display:none"><i> I received this ARC from 47North Amazon Publishing Via NG in return for an honest review.</i><br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Deep down, however, I fear that I’ve come to love a lie.”</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>Bruised…battered….gutted…in shock. Those are my feelings right now!</b><br /><br />Amy Bartol I’m breaking up with you<br /><br />You led me astray.<br /><br />You gave me mixed signals.<br /><br />I trusted you!<br /><br />I trusted you with my heart and you smashed it with your words. <br /><br />How could you?<br /><br />If we were married, I’d want a divorce.<br /><br />How could you take away the boys? How could you take Jax, Trey and Wayra away from me? <br /><br />*takes a shuddering breath*<br /><br />Those first two books, were some of the happiest and most glorious books of my life.<br /><br />Why did you do it? <br /><br />Wasn’t my love enough?<br /><br />Didn’t you know how much I loved Kricket? <br /><br />You made her into someone else! <br /><br />I thought you understood where this was going and boy, did I want it to be real! *starts crying*<br /><br />You ruined me! And demolished my soul with a wrecking ball. Thanks a lot!<br /><br />WE’RE OVER!<br /><br />*cough* Sorry about that! I’m going to try to be very objective here and ugh…cast my feelings aside for just a moment <s>though I didn’t exactly do a great job of it at the start</s><br /><br />Let’s talk about the plot<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>Kyon finally has Kricket in his grasp,<br /><br />Lies are brought forth.<br /><br />Plots unconcealed.<br /><br />Lives destroyed. <br /><br />Not anyone are who they say they are, and things are not as they seem.<br /><br />Certainty and love are at war. <br /><br />And sometimes the lines are blurred between lover and enemy.<br /><br />An Empress will rise if the land of Ethar,<br /><br />But first we must darken the stars. </i>
</blockquote><br /><br />Actual rating…2.5 Stars. <br /><br />This is hard for me guys. I battled with not rating it as a 1 star, because, trying to be objective here- the <br />writing was still amazing…the plot was complex.<br /><br />Oh heck, objectivity is over.<br /><br />WHAT THE HECK HAPPENED HERE?<br /><br />*tread careful from this point, potential spoilers below, read at thine own risk!*<br /><br />I had more of a hate than love relationship with this book. <br /><br />Now the first book was near perfect to me I gave it a 4.5 stars, the second was a knock out and I gave it a straight 5 stars, heck I’d give it a 6 star out of 5. This one's rating halves the last book! <br /><br />What happened? Why did you take away Trey? How could you try to make me like Kyon?<br /> <br />What did you do with Kricket? Was it demon possession? Was she abducted and replaced by aliens? <br /><br />Why did she do a 180? Why was she so different? <br /><br />Why did the plot change so much!!? <br /><br />Make me understand! <br /><br />Was this all a vision that Kricket was having and all this didn’t actually happen? Tell me that’s what’s happening, please! <br /><br />61% of this book was like a honeymoon of Kyon and Kricket! Again, what the heck?<br /><br />Warning:- Mother of all love triangles here!<br /><br />Trey! How could you Bartol? I know it’s within your author rights, but I loved the man! (Don’t worry guys, he’s not dead) but Bartol! He made it into my book-boyfriend list and I hardly got any Trey in my life this time! Why? <br /><br />I know this review is full of questions, I feel played, used and cheated.<br /> <br />And I’m bitter for it. <br /><br />I felt everything so keenly, which is why I knew I couldn’t just rate it a 1 star. You got me good Bartol. You got me good. You pulverized my soul. <br /><br />Ladies and Gents…this book is nothing like what we expected and while this may work for some, it…wrecked me. <br /><br />It’s a good book. But I thought the story would go a different way. I had hoped it would go a different way. Bartol if you wanted to show the harsh realities of life well played. <br /><br /><b>Be prepared to be shocked everyone! I certainly was!</b><br /> <br />I’m so confused about everything here. So many feelings. <br /><br />Kricket…was one of my favourite characters of all time. This book made me feel murderous…towards her!<br /><br />Is this the last book? Could it just end like that? Surely not…right?<br /><br />I’ll stop right there, I can’t go on. <br /><br />Stay awesome! <br /><br />-The Book Herald<br /><br /><i>Tweet me <a href="https://twitter.com/TheBookHerald" rel="nofollow noopener">@thebookherald</a></i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4465901856153327788"><i>2.5 damn the stars</i><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I'm a watercolor, bleeding luminosity in smearing swirls of sorrow.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451372217i/17534802._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Really pains me to say this, but I just can't... this third installment took a turn down a road that unfortunately didn't work for me. It has nothing to do with the authors style or skill, just the series of events that occurred in this last installment that just had me wondering if I was still reading the same series. <b>Darken The Stars</b> was a slower paced book while the first two were action packed an</span>
  <span id="freeText4465901856153327788" style="display:none"><i>2.5 damn the stars</i><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I'm a watercolor, bleeding luminosity in smearing swirls of sorrow.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451372217i/17534802._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Really pains me to say this, but I just can't... this third installment took a turn down a road that unfortunately didn't work for me. It has nothing to do with the authors style or skill, just the series of events that occurred in this last installment that just had me wondering if I was still reading the same series. <b>Darken The Stars</b> was a slower paced book while the first two were action packed and full of hope and a future so bright, I guess I should have headed the title of this as a warning, because the stars were indeed darkened. I was heavily invested in this series and I take full responsibility for my having my expectations too high. All the characters took roles I never imagined them taking, and having lived with them, knowing them and seeing what made them tick for two whole books, it was hard to swallow the change in persona. While this was the end, I'm hoping it's an end for now, because while this may not have worked for me, I'd like to think that there is more a possibility of more...<br> <br><i>ARC kindly provided by 47North , via NetGalley, in exchange for an honest review.</i><br> <br>***Quotes above are taken from the ARC version of the book and may differ upon publication.<br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_1353333899" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1353333899" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1353333899?book_show_action=true">Aug 03, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=5-stars-favorites">5-stars-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=6-stars-top-favorites">6-stars-top-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1353333899" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1422654251731866590"><b>6 Kyon oh My Stars</b><br/><br/>Darken the Stars is the third novel in the Kricket Series. <br/><br/>I love this series like crazy mad. I love it so much that after I finished reading Darken the Stars, I went ahead and did an audio re-read of the first book, Under Different Stars, I just had to get my fix AGAIN.<br/><br/>You will have to read this series in order, but let me just say … and this is for those who haven’t read the series… you will be awed, delighted and consumed by this read. Amy A. Bartol knows how to write a good</span>
  <span id="freeText1422654251731866590" style="display:none"><b>6 Kyon oh My Stars</b><br><br>Darken the Stars is the third novel in the Kricket Series. <br><br>I love this series like crazy mad. I love it so much that after I finished reading Darken the Stars, I went ahead and did an audio re-read of the first book, Under Different Stars, I just had to get my fix AGAIN.<br><br>You will have to read this series in order, but let me just say … and this is for those who haven’t read the series… you will be awed, delighted and consumed by this read. Amy A. Bartol knows how to write a good fantasy book. I would label this as young adult, but it’s steamier than your normal YA novel. It has everything I look for in a YA read, with intrigue, action and crazy love tension. <br><br>You know it’s a good series, when there’s a love triangle and I LOVEEE IT!!!!!<br><br>If you have read the first two books and you are on the fence about this one, DO NOT BE. You must read this one. It’s a treat and it’s my favorite so far. <br><br>Darken the Stars picks up RIGHT where Sea of Stars left off, I’m talking nano-seconds from where it left off, so you will not be confused at all. Kyon now has Kricket and A LOT of questions are on my mind. <br><br><b>What will Kyon do with Kricket?</b><br><br><b>What will Kricket do? </b><br><br><b>How will Trey react? </b><br><br>So many questions… I don’t want to give anything away, but I will say, I’ve been a Kyon fan from the start. Don’t get me wrong, I love Trey, but there’s something about Kyon’s obsession towards Kricket that has left me … with a little crush towards him. I love Kyon because he’s so dominate, ruthless and he will do ANYTHING to have Kricket.<br><br>I’m also partial to crazy killers.<br><br>Darken the Stars is heavily focused on Kyon. It will show you many sides of him and kind of open to who he is, what he does and why he does the things he does. I REALLY ENJOYED IT. I also love being in Kricket’s mind. She has such a complex. She needs to keep the peace, protect her sister, her loved ones and even her heart.<br><br>I love Kricket even more in this book because she remains focus and strong. There are so many factors that come to play in this book. I love how everyone is linked together. Gah, I couldn’t get enough. I read this in one sitting and stayed up till 1am until I finished! I never do that.<br><br><b>It’s an amazing book and an amazing series. I’m in love. </b><br><br>NOTE: The author has a three book contract with the publisher. As of this moment, there is no deal for a fourth book, HOWEVER that can change. I have a feeling that the forth book will be in the works fairly soon.<br><br><br><i>An ARC was provided</i><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/19504931.Under_Different_Stars__Kricket___1_" title="Under Different Stars (Kricket, #1) by Amy A. Bartol" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1394758272s/19504931.jpg" alt="Under Different Stars (Kricket, #1) by Amy A. Bartol" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_1263124083" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1263124083" />
    <a title="Aira  Cabrera" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6021566-aira-cabrera"><img alt="Aira  Cabrera" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420132998p2/6021566.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1263124083?book_show_action=true">Apr 24, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aira  Cabrera" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aira  Cabrera" href="/user/show/6021566-aira-cabrera">Aira  Cabrera</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1263124083" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3294887553330037014"><i>ARC received from the publisher via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review.</i><br/><br/>This book blew me away. It was better than the first and second book. This just had more depth to it, and I felt more for the characters. I don’t know how I’m going to explain all my feelings about this book. Trust me, I was a mess while reading this.<br/><br/>Kyon finally has Kricket. This guy got her, then lost her, got her, then lost her. I wish I had his determination. I know that Kyon’s not really a good guy; but I like hi</span>
  <span id="freeText3294887553330037014" style="display:none"><i>ARC received from the publisher via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review.</i><br><br>This book blew me away. It was better than the first and second book. This just had more depth to it, and I felt more for the characters. I don’t know how I’m going to explain all my feelings about this book. Trust me, I was a mess while reading this.<br><br>Kyon finally has Kricket. This guy got her, then lost her, got her, then lost her. I wish I had his determination. I know that Kyon’s not really a good guy; but I like him. Yeah, I lost my marbles. In the first and second book, I just liked him, now I love him. He really did love Kricket. Sure, he was extremely possessive , but it was because of how he was raised. He scared me, and I liked him, but I didn’t really want him with Kricket in the end, because I thought he was unstable. He changed though. He really did. He was still extremely possessive, but not in a scary way anymore. Okay, I’m talking so much about him, moving on.<br><br>Kricket now has new enemies, and even greater problems. Her supposed allies, were even her enemies. Everyone wants her dead, except for a few people. You’ll be surprised who wants her dead. They didn’t really say it, but it was obvious. It broke my heart. I felt so bad for Kricket. Her existence is basically only for the use of others. I wanted to give her a hug.<br><br>Trey. Oh no. I don’t even know what to say about him. I love him, I really do, but he made mistakes in this book. I don’t know how I feel about him anymore. I want to hug him, but I also want to punch him in the face.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419397939ra/13057442.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kricket’s father is supposed to be the good guy, and he is the good guy for some, but I don’t really agree with them. He cares for one daughter, and doesn’t give a shit about the other. I don’t care what the future entails and all that crap. You don’t do that to your child. Kricket’s father is a fucking douchcanoe. I wanted to murder this guy! He’s fucking useless and he’s heartless. Just a reminder for Kricket’s father.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439021308ra/15783075.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book was just really intense for me. It was awesome, but I was scared to turn pages. Kricket really didn’t need any more problems.<br><br>This was supposed to be a trilogy, but I just cannot accept that ending. I thought I was being punked, but then I remembered that no one really knows who I am besides my family. If the author decides that this will be the last book, I will die. Not literally, in case you were wondering. Nope, this is not the end. I refuse to accept that ending. Do you guys know how many times I cried while reading?! Too many to mention. It’s not even a sad book!!! I mean, some parts were really sad, but I usually don’t cry this much. I’m too emotionally invested in this series. I need to read or watch something really happy to get over this.<br><br> <a href="https://airareads.wordpress.com/2015/08/08/review-darken-the-stars-kricket-3-by-amy-a-bartol/" rel="nofollow noopener">BLOG POST</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="3294887553330037014" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1349625288?book_show_action=true">Jul 30, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/26253159-darken-the-stars">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=dangerous-hero-themed-books-read">dangerous-hero-themed-books-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=love-triangles">love-triangles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=hate-that-i-love-them">hate-that-i-love-them</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=sweet-heart-warming-stories">sweet-heart-warming-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=arcs">arcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=shocking-twists">shocking-twists</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1349625288" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5913120554872528862">***I received a complimentary ARC of this book from the publisher, through Netgalley.com, in exchange for honest feedback.***<br/><br/>After finishing this book, I feel so conflicted. It definitely didn't end the way I had envisioned. As much as I loved the unpredictable plot twists, I can't say that I ever fully caught up with the twists and turns. I'm emotionally "stuck" in book 2 and I couldn't really move forward. I guess I just don't adjust to change all that well. Here I had Kricket's entire future </span>
  <span id="freeText5913120554872528862" style="display:none">***I received a complimentary ARC of this book from the publisher, through Netgalley.com, in exchange for honest feedback.***<br /><br />After finishing this book, I feel so conflicted. It definitely didn't end the way I had envisioned. As much as I loved the unpredictable plot twists, I can't say that I ever fully caught up with the twists and turns. I'm emotionally "stuck" in book 2 and I couldn't really move forward. I guess I just don't adjust to change all that well. Here I had Kricket's entire future mapped out for her, and it ended up being nothing like I had imagined. I'm gutted!<br /><br />That being said, this book was another exceptional story. The characters continue to captivate me. Kyon, in particular, proved to be multidimensional and had far more depth than was revealed in the earlier books. This book was his chance to shine and he did not disappoint!<br /><br />On the other hand, I found myself disappointed in Trey and, at times, Kricket. Both of them seemed to treat their love as a passing fancy, disposable and easily forgotten. I always want the "original" couple to stay together in my love stories, so I struggle anytime that there is any perceived fallibility on that front. Needless to say, I had a lot of mixed feelings when the dynamics of Kricket's love life began to change.<br /><br />The ending was shocking to me, but somehow fitting. I felt heartbroken for Kricket and can't blame her for the path that she chose. I'm still not sure how I'd like to see it end, especially after seeing another side to Kyon and Trey. I just know that this book left me feeling gutted. <br /><br />I want Kricket to get her HEA and I just don't feel like that happened here. However, this book was left wide open for another book in the series. I'm hoping that there will be one shortly to tie up these loose ends and provide some closure. At this point, Kricket got a bum deal.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5913120554872528862" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1279157608" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1279157608" />
    <a title="Whitney Mcgregor (A Literary Perusal)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3620574-whitney-mcgregor-a-literary-perusal"><img alt="Whitney Mcgregor (A Literary Perusal)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1381168770p2/3620574.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1279157608?book_show_action=true">May 13, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Whitney Mcgregor (A Literary Perusal)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Whitney Mcgregor (A Literary Perusal)" href="/user/show/3620574-whitney-mcgregor-a-literary-perusal">Whitney Mcgregor (A Literary Perusal)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1279157608" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18323021982767067046">This may be the hardest review I've ever written. It actually breaks my heart to only give this book two stars because I love Amy and I've loved the series up to this point. <br/><br/>There were things I enjoyed about this story. Kricket is amazing as usual and I totally fell for Kyon. There are some tough moments where Kricket makes some decisions readers may not like. I think she did what she needed to do to survive though. <br/><br/>Amy's writing is fun and the magical world she created for this series really co</span>
  <span id="freeText18323021982767067046" style="display:none">This may be the hardest review I've ever written. It actually breaks my heart to only give this book two stars because I love Amy and I've loved the series up to this point. <br /><br />There were things I enjoyed about this story. Kricket is amazing as usual and I totally fell for Kyon. There are some tough moments where Kricket makes some decisions readers may not like. I think she did what she needed to do to survive though. <br /><br />Amy's writing is fun and the magical world she created for this series really comes alive on the pages. <br /><br />It's almost impossible to go into detail without revealing spoilers so I'll just be honest and say my problem is with the ending. I hit about 75% in and got a very bad feeling. I kept swiping the pages praying for more when it was over and my heart was just crushed. <br /><br />To be so invested in the series and the characters, I was quite disappointed with the direction the story went and I feel a bit cheated to be honest. It seems all of the character and plot development just kind of got thrown away. <br /><br />This is/was billed as trilogy and if I knew there were going to be more books, my rating would be much higher than two stars. But as a trilogy, this has left me unsatisfied and I am keeping my fingers crossed that the publisher will approve more books. I honestly think Amy could get two more books out of this series and I would love that! I want more of these characters and more of their story. <br /><br />So while my review probably seems harsh, it's very honest. Love the characters, love the first two books, love the author's writing but the end of this book ruined the story for me. If this is all there will be, I will leave this series wishing I hadn't started it. </span>
  <a data-text-id="18323021982767067046" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1381541745" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1381541745" />
    <a title="Vilma Iris" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15777655-vilma-iris"><img alt="Vilma Iris" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1501855386p2/15777655.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1381541745" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14188163157827885014">Sadly, I didn't connect with this book. The plot went in a direction I didn't understand and it felt abrupt. The protagonists made decisions that felt out of character and I found myself heartbroken and lost. Amy is an amazing storyteller and I've loved everything she's put out there until now. I know she will come back even stronger, especially as we anxiously await Iniquity.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1201988296" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1201988296" />
    <a title="Stacee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7359586-stacee"><img alt="Stacee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577910954p2/7359586.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1201988296?book_show_action=true">Feb 15, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacee" href="/user/show/7359586-stacee">Stacee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7359586-stacee?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7359586-stacee?shelf=theyre-tattoos-not-ink-or-tats">theyre-tattoos-not-ink-or-tats</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7359586-stacee?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7359586-stacee?shelf=dont-cheat">dont-cheat</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1201988296" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4000877350720338089">Well, first off I will say that I read the ending of this first, like I do with any trilogy ending and I was quite upset by it. In turn, that made me lose all excitement for reading the book. But then I picked it up and was absolutely blown away. <br/><br/>The other thing I will mention is that I was 100% Team Trey, but after this book, my undying devotion is 1000% Team Kyon. There is so much more to Kyon than what we saw in the first two books. He is swoony as fuck and so so so smitten by Kricket that it</span>
  <span id="freeText4000877350720338089" style="display:none">Well, first off I will say that I read the ending of this first, like I do with any trilogy ending and I was quite upset by it. In turn, that made me lose all excitement for reading the book. But then I picked it up and was absolutely blown away. <br /><br />The other thing I will mention is that I was 100% Team Trey, but after this book, my undying devotion is 1000% Team Kyon. There is so much more to Kyon than what we saw in the first two books. He is swoony as fuck and so so so smitten by Kricket that it's near impossible not to love him. Not to mention Kyon teaches her things, confides in her, and sees her as an equal, to stand beside him. Trey only wanted to stand in front of her, doing what he thought was best. <br /><br />And now Kricket. She's still the snarky, strong girl she has been from the beginning. I love what she did in this book and the choices she went with. There's a side of playfulness I wasn't expecting and really, I just couldn't get enough of her and Kyon together. <br /><br />That ending that I was bitching about? Yeah, it really works. I absolutely feel like it's open enough for another book, but if we don't ever get one, I've happily concocted the exact HEA that I want. That being said, I ABSOLUTELY WANT MORE. <br /><br />**Huge thanks to 47North and NetGalley for providing the arc in exchange for an honest review**<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4000877350720338089" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText14337624847181462124" style="display:none">There's a lot of controversy with this book. And while I can see why some readers aren't happy with the end--I agree, this can't be the end for Kricket--I never read this series as ONLY a romance. (Although I DO appreciate the romance in the story.) To me, this story has always been about KRICKET--discovering her true identity, learning who to trust. Kricket has grown into herself and become stronger for it. <br /><br />If you're reading this series to see who she ends up with at the end, this may not make you happy. But if you're reading this because you recognize Kricket as the survivor she's always been, I think you'll enjoy it. And let's hope Amy will soon announce when she'll release book four. </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1350536367?book_show_action=true">Jul 31, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shelley" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shelley" href="/user/show/10797120-shelley">Shelley</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10797120-shelley?shelf=just-got-my-arc">just-got-my-arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1350536367" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10159380679995001278">5+ Baw-da-Baw Stars<br/><br/>11-9-20<br/>Just read this series again for the ++++time. Every time I finish it leaves me wanting more. I NEED to know what happens to all these characters. The more I read it the more I see the characters in different lights. Once you know what happens in the end, reading the first ones again I see Kyon throughout the series for what he really is. It is so hard bc I love Trey and Kyon, but lets face it Kyon is her true match. Kricket breaks my heart. For someone who was raised wi</span>
  <span id="freeText10159380679995001278" style="display:none">5+ Baw-da-Baw Stars<br><br>11-9-20<br>Just read this series again for the ++++time. Every time I finish it leaves me wanting more. I NEED to know what happens to all these characters. The more I read it the more I see the characters in different lights. Once you know what happens in the end, reading the first ones again I see Kyon throughout the series for what he really is. It is so hard bc I love Trey and Kyon, but lets face it Kyon is her true match. Kricket breaks my heart. For someone who was raised without love, she shows it to all those in her life, even when they don't deserve it. I have to admit I would love to see Pan and Giffin get some of what they deserve. <br><br>ARC generously provided by publisher via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review. <br><br>How I feel about Amy Bartol and all her books!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435677636ra/15369957.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Darken the Stars</i> takes off right where <i> Sea of Stars</i> leaves off. Kricket finds herself in Kyon's possession, torn away from her love, Trey, and forced into a world that wants her dead. Kricket continues to fight what she knows is right and uses her gift to help her do it. Kricket continues to be such a strong lead character and there are lots of surprises with characters that you think you know but you really don't.<br><br><br>There is so much I want to say about this book, but since I was lucky enough to receive an ARC for this book I do not want to give anything away for those who have yet to read it. I will say I have loved Trey from the start and have been torn because Kyon is suppose to be a bad guy and someone you aren't suppose to like but just can't seem to help yourself. Yes Kyon is on the "bad side" but he has proven himself to not be a bad guy especially where Kricket is concerned. So it is so easy to identify with Kricket through out this book.<br><br>Once I picked up this book I did not want to put it down. I couldn't wait to find out what was going to happen and then when it was over found myself so sad that this is the last in the series. <br><br>Now I refuse to give anything away about this book but I will say I was surprised by the ending. Actually I am not sure how I feel about the ending. I understand it and it completely makes sense to me, and it actually gives me hope that maybe Ms. Bartol might write another story about these characters because it is possible. However it is not the HEA I was looking for or wanting. In the end everyone gets what they want, well everyone but Kricket, her whole life has been about sacrifice and continues to be that way. It is just one more thing that makes her such an amazing character. (Personally I really wanted Giffen and Pan to get some sort of hurt for all they have done to Kricket, alas I am left wondering). I would love to read what happens to all these characters in the future, one can hope!</span>

<div id="review_1230387336" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1230387336" />
    <a title="Mlpmom (Book Reviewer)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3829694-mlpmom-book-reviewer"><img alt="Mlpmom (Book Reviewer)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1375481031p2/3829694.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1230387336?book_show_action=true">Mar 17, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mlpmom (Book Reviewer)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mlpmom (Book Reviewer)" href="/user/show/3829694-mlpmom-book-reviewer">Mlpmom (Book Reviewer)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3829694-mlpmom-book-reviewer?shelf=kindle-books">kindle-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3829694-mlpmom-book-reviewer?shelf=arc-book-read">arc-book-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1230387336" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1056430344246585410">Amy Bartol has done something that I didn't ever think possible, she made me fall in love with a genre that before now, I never really paid much attention to. Not because I didn't like it necessarily, but because I just never had any interest in it until now.<br/><br/>She managed to capture my attention from the very first book in the series and not only hold it, but with book two, be in love with it. I couldn't put her books down and devoured them all. To say I have been anxiously awaiting the release of</span>
  <span id="freeText1056430344246585410" style="display:none">Amy Bartol has done something that I didn't ever think possible, she made me fall in love with a genre that before now, I never really paid much attention to. Not because I didn't like it necessarily, but because I just never had any interest in it until now.<br /><br />She managed to capture my attention from the very first book in the series and not only hold it, but with book two, be in love with it. I couldn't put her books down and devoured them all. To say I have been anxiously awaiting the release of book three, is quite the understatement. <br /><br />Kricket, Jax, Trey, Wayra and yes, even Griffen and Kyon stole my heart with each new book and I have become so invested in their stories that I just knew this last book, would be epic.<br /><br />It is never easy reading the last book in a series. You want to devour it at the same time that you want to savor it and if you are anything like me, you war with yourself on which you should do. In the case of Darken the Stars, I had to devour it, I didn't have any other choice. Once I picked it up, I was immediately whisked right back into Kricket's world and I didn't want to leave until her story was over and I was hoping like heck, that however it ended, it would be a good one. One that would finally give Kricket some peace and hopefully happiness and love too. <br /><br />This book played with my emotions more than any of the others have. I was torn between those characters I already loved and cared about, to liking characters and even loving certain characters, that I never looked twice at or thought I would actually feel for, let alone grow to care and love.<br /><br />The story took unexpected twists and turns that I wasn't quite ready for. Kricket is in a tough position no matter what she chooses and like always, she has to look out for those that she cares about as well as trying to keep herself safe and protected. There is no easy choice for her. <br /><br />There is no easy road for her to go on. No matter what, I knew someone was going to get hurt and I thought I would be prepared for that. <br /><br />My emotions are still all over the place with the ending and honestly, I'm not going to say a whole lot about it other than Bartol made it realistic to the rest of the storyline, to who Kricket has always been throughout the series and for that, I am thankful for it. Was it the one I was expecting? Not. At. All. <br />But that's okay too, I'm happy with the way it all went down and especially with the fact that with the ending the way it was, I could definitely see a spin off or even a sequel come about eventually. <br /><br />All in all, a very realistic and believable conclusion to the series.<br /><br /><br />*An ARC Copy of this was provided by the Publisher in exchange for an honest review.*</span>
  <a data-text-id="1056430344246585410" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2069846442" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2069846442" />
    <a title="Ashlee » Library In The Country" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7990992-ashlee-library-in-the-country"><img alt="Ashlee » Library In The Country" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597652881p2/7990992.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2069846442?book_show_action=true">Jul 24, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ashlee » Library In The Country" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ashlee » Library In The Country" href="/user/show/7990992-ashlee-library-in-the-country">Ashlee » Library In The Country</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25277389-darken-the-stars">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7990992-ashlee-library-in-the-country?shelf=owned-paperback">owned-paperback</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7990992-ashlee-library-in-the-country?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7990992-ashlee-library-in-the-country?shelf=sci-fi-read">sci-fi-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7990992-ashlee-library-in-the-country?shelf=urban-fantasy-read">urban-fantasy-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2069846442" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16704391556827179042">4.5 (This review may have some mild spoilers, but nothing explicitly stated.)<br/><br/>What can I say about this book? First of all, I am writing this review about three months after having originally read it and am so happy I waited. I found myself with a terrible book hangover after finishing this. I loved it, but also wasn't sure what to think of it and really just needed to give myself time to process it. After some time, I really feel differently about it than I did when I first finished.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"I think </i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText16704391556827179042" style="display:none">4.5 (This review may have some mild spoilers, but nothing explicitly stated.)<br /><br />What can I say about this book? First of all, I am writing this review about three months after having originally read it and am so happy I waited. I found myself with a terrible book hangover after finishing this. I loved it, but also wasn't sure what to think of it and really just needed to give myself time to process it. After some time, I really feel differently about it than I did when I first finished.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"I think I’m the most hurt by the fact that I’m not like him. I would’ve chosen him over everything else. The whole world could’ve burned down and I would’ve pulled him from the wreckage of it."</i>
</b><br /><br />Let me start by saying that this book does not have the pace of the previous two books in the least. Additionally, there is a certain male character that I came to love immensely that does not have as big of a role in this installment as he did in the previous two. At first I found myself very frustrated by this as he was my favorite character in the series and I just wanted more and more of him. Looking back, I do still wish we had more of a look at what he was doing throughout this story when he wasn't present. I really found myself questioning his actions and motives and would love more insight into his mind and what he was thinking at the time. Needless to say, it felt a little personal, as if someone had broken a promise to me. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>"I found her. I lost her. I found her. I lost her. I found her."</i>
</b><br /><br />On the other hand, there is another male character we get a WHOLE LOT OF. A whole lot I did not want or desire initially, but Bartol really knows how to make you go from loving to hate a character to wanting to love them. This is exactly how I felt. Now, let me also make a reference to this character's history throughout the story. He has done some really horrible things and despite the explanations in this story for his actions, I did not feel like they were excusable at all. On the other hand, I still grew to have feelings for him as the story progressed and felt myself even pitying and rooting for him at times. One cannot deny that him and Kricket would make a ruthless and powerful team, as this installment hints at. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Deep down, however, I fear that I’ve come to love a lie."</i>
</b><br /><br />Now, onto Kricket herself. It is apparent that Kricket is not the same person she was when this story started. Where are her loyalties? As this story progresses, its clear that Kricket's heart and mind are at war with each other and she is trying hard to understand who can be trusted and who does not have her best interests at heart. Those she was certain would always support her aren't around and those she told herself to guard against are willing to do anything for her, even if they didn't intend for that to happen either. However, perhaps Kricket hasn't changed as much as it appears. The most important person in Kricket's life is herself and at the end of the day she must make the choice that is best for her and so that's exactly what she does. With a little bit of revenge, cunning and fury tossed in there too.<br /><br />The ending to this story was not at all what I expected. I am not a "must have my HEA!" type person, but this ending really took me by surprise and left me feeling a little unsettled. I totally support and understand Kricket's choice, but I also wish there could have been another way. <br /><br />Now, if you read this and are wanting more, take a stroll over to Bartol's blog as there is a little sampling of what could be a progression of this story and why she has not published more (at this point). That being said, I feel like there is so much more to be told about this story - Kricket, Trey, Kyon, Ethar &amp; Earth, our boys Jax and Wayra, Charisma and Trey's family, Giffen and Astrid and more. I don't want to be one of THOSE people but if any series could continue past where it was meant to end, this one would be my choice. (I hope you're reading this, 47North!)<br /><br />At the end of the day, despite the ending taking me by surprise, this is still one of my all-time favorite series and one I will continue to cherish as time goes on.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16704391556827179042" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1200234639" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1200234639" />
    <a title="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11672704-donna-the-romance-cover"><img alt="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1369044455p2/11672704.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1200234639?book_show_action=true">Feb 14, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" href="/user/show/11672704-donna-the-romance-cover">Donna ~ The Romance Cover</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11672704-donna-the-romance-cover?shelf=4-star-reads-2015">4-star-reads-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1200234639" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15172331419074348128">Darken the Stars (Kricket #3) by Amy Bartol<br/>4 stars!!	<br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“The stars are no longer aligning for me; they’re bleeding from the sky, turning black, and dying around me. What the people in this room don’t realize is that I’m not the one.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/>This is the final book of this series and what an ending. This is one of those books that I cannot give any details away, literally, none. Everything is a spoiler. This is also one of those books whereby for once I am demanding more and not just a “I’m being</span>
  <span id="freeText15172331419074348128" style="display:none">Darken the Stars (Kricket #3) by Amy Bartol<br />4 stars!!	<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“The stars are no longer aligning for me; they’re bleeding from the sky, turning black, and dying around me. What the people in this room don’t realize is that I’m not the one.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />This is the final book of this series and what an ending. This is one of those books that I cannot give any details away, literally, none. Everything is a spoiler. This is also one of those books whereby for once I am demanding more and not just a “I’m being greedy, I want more”. This is the first case I have come across where the characters demand more, this story still has a lot of legs and while I appreciate and understand the way this finished, for me personally as soon as I had finished, I had already plotted out the next book. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Baw-da-baw.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />This is also the first time I have sobbed at the ending of a book just because it had finished. Once I had got a hold of myself I sat there and thought “why on earth are you crying woman?” The only thing I could come up with is because I didn’t feel closure; this just couldn’t be the end. The trouble with Amy Bartol is she has a knack of endearing her characters to you on all levels, these characters become a piece of you and because she goes into so much depth you know how and what these characters would do in certain circumstances. I know what should happen, I just hope that the publishers take into account my pleading and option a fourth book. I need to know that these characters are okay after everything they have been through. I just want more...PLEASE!!!<br /><br />This is my first dystopian series and a genre that I do not typically read but such is the power of Amy Bartol’s draw that I had to give it a go just because I loved her Premonition series so much. I had tried to read this genre in the past but just couldn’t gel with it, but somehow Amy Bartol managed to draw me into this world and made me not only love it, but want more of it. <br /><br />This final book is about war, the fight for survival, love, trust, betrayal and the most overwhelming fear I have ever had while reading. Fear for these characters, fear for what I thought I knew, fear for actions I never thought I would read about, just shock, horror and confusion but more importantly I understood, everything. While this was not what I was expecting, I could see the whys and wherefores, after all, what we the reader need to remember is that this is Kricket’s story. Kricket's sole aim is to survive and thrive and this is definitely her story.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I’m stone. I’m stone. I’m stone.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />I found myself loving those I hated and hating those I loved, something that I thought was impossible. With this kind of read you cannot help but move your thoughts ahead a mile a minute and plotting and scheming as to what you want to happen and what you hope would happen, so it when it doesn’t pan out that way you are actually taken aback.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“That’s because you only served to convince me that you’re perfect for me. My little savage – the darkest star.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />Overall, this is one series that I will never forget and one that when I need an escape from reality I will definitely be reading again. I have to applaud Amy Bartol on once again her creativeness and her imagination. Her flair for totally immersing you into her “worlds” so effortlessly only goes to show what a unique talent she has. I also have to applaud her courage in delivering a book that she wanted, the direction that she envisioned her characters taking. While it may not be what we all wanted or expected, kudos to her. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“It’s not alone. It has the world.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />So 47North, my last ditch plea...I need another book, seriously. Not just a maybe, but a definitely.<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.theromancecover.com">www.theromancecover.com</a><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15172331419074348128" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Bartol, because you have done what very few are capable of... making me love a love triangle. I dove into this book expecting greatness and I was not disappointed.
